The dam's reservoir is 666km long and has an average width of 1km.\nThe electricity generated is enough to meet 10% of China's electricity demand.\nChina spent 37 billion dollars to build the Three Gorges Dam.\n\n2. Pearl River Delta - Huge megacity\nThe Pearl River Delta is made up of 9 cities including: Shenzhen, Dongguan, Huizhou, Zhongshan, Zhuhai, Jiangmen, Guangzhou, Foshan and Zhaoqing. China has combined them into giant megacities.\nWith an area as large as Croatia (56,594 km2) and a population equal to the entire Turkey (85,279,553 people), it is planned that by 2030 China will pour about 322 billion dollars to build infrastructure in this area.\nIn 2023, the GDP of this megacity is 1.4 billion dollars, equivalent to the GDP of Indonesia.\n\n3. Daxing International Airport - Beijing.\nIt is one of the largest airports in the world with a total investment of 17 billion dollars. H\u1ea7u h\u1ebft c\u00e1c blockchain ph\u1ed5 bi\u1ebfn nh\u01b0 Bitcoin v\u00e0 Ethereum \u0111\u1ec1u l\u01b0u tr\u1eef th\u00f4ng tin c\u00f3 gi\u00e1 tr\u1ecb v\u1ec1 c\u00e1c lo\u1ea1i t\u00e0i s\u1ea3n trong m\u1ea1ng l\u01b0\u1edbi.\n\nV\u00ed d\u1ee5: Khi ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng s\u1edf h\u1eefu NFT, si\u00eau d\u1eef li\u1ec7u \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c li\u00ean k\u1ebft bao g\u1ed3m th\u00f4ng tin chi ti\u1ebft v\u1ec1 t\u00e1c ph\u1ea9m ngh\u1ec7 thu\u1eadt k\u1ef9 thu\u1eadt s\u1ed1, ng\u01b0\u1eddi t\u1ea1o, l\u1ecbch s\u1eed quy\u1ec1n s\u1edf h\u1eefu th\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c li\u00ean k\u1ebft v\u1edbi NFT \u0111\u00f3.\n\nNgo\u00e0i ra, ng\u01b0\u1eddi d\u00f9ng giao d\u1ecbch Bitcoin c\u0169ng c\u00f3 th\u1ec3 mang si\u00eau d\u1eef li\u1ec7u bao g\u1ed3m d\u1eef li\u1ec7u kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c m\u00e3 h\u00f3a.
